\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} represents an isolated instance of the \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} engine. \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} isolates have completely separate states. Objects from one isolate must not be used in other isolates. The embedder can create multiple isolates and use them in parallel in multiple threads. An isolate can be entered by at most one thread at any given time. The Locker/\+Unlocker API must be used to synchronize. 

\doxysubsection{Member Typedef Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_ad08ef7777576edf86a99c3d4130a34d6}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_ad08ef7777576edf86a99c3d4130a34d6}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!AbortOnUncaughtExceptionCallback@{AbortOnUncaughtExceptionCallback}}
\index{AbortOnUncaughtExceptionCallback@{AbortOnUncaughtExceptionCallback}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AbortOnUncaughtExceptionCallback}{AbortOnUncaughtExceptionCallback}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily using \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_ad08ef7777576edf86a99c3d4130a34d6}{v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Abort\+On\+Uncaught\+Exception\+Callback}} =  bool ($\ast$)(\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}}$\ast$)}

Custom callback used by embedders to help \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} determine if it should abort when it throws and no internal handler is predicted to catch the exception. If --abort-\/on-\/uncaught-\/exception is used on the command line, then \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} will abort if either\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item no custom callback is set.
\item the custom callback set returns true. Otherwise, the custom callback will not be called and \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} will not abort. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a6607ff094036df195e81565edc86badd}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a6607ff094036df195e81565edc86badd}}

\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!TimeZoneDetection@{TimeZoneDetection}}
\index{TimeZoneDetection@{TimeZoneDetection}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{TimeZoneDetection}{TimeZoneDetection}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_a57dcf1e56d6498b7426ef7a489454ffe}{v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Time\+Zone\+Detection}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}

Time zone redetection indicator for Date\+Time\+Configuration\+Change\+Notification.

k\+Skip indicates \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} that the notification should not trigger redetecting host time zone. k\+Redetect indicates \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} that host time zone should be redetected, and used to set the default time zone.

The host time zone detection may require file system access or similar operations unlikely to be available inside a sandbox. If \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8}{v8}} is run inside a sandbox, the host time zone has to be detected outside the sandbox before calling Date\+Time\+Configuration\+Change\+Notification function. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{kSkip@{kSkip}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!kSkip@{kSkip}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a57dcf1e56d6498b7426ef7a489454ffeac88bd8ce07240b0611d5ae619c1aa088}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a57dcf1e56d6498b7426ef7a489454ffeac88bd8ce07240b0611d5ae619c1aa088}} 
k\+Skip&\\

{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_aed6909379c3f2820cb3084710b73385d}{v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Use\+Counter\+Feature}}}

Features reported via the Set\+Use\+Counter\+Callback callback. Do not change assigned numbers of existing items; add new features to the end of this list. Dead features can be marked {\ttfamily V8\+\_\+\+DEPRECATE\+\_\+\+SOON}, then {\ttfamily V8\+\_\+\+DEPRECATED}, and then finally be renamed to {\ttfamily k\+OBSOLETE\+\_\+...} to stop embedders from using them. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

\index{AddBeforeCallEnteredCallback@{AddBeforeCallEnteredCallback}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AddBeforeCallEnteredCallback()}{AddBeforeCallEnteredCallback()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Add\+Before\+Call\+Entered\+Callback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_aa724c4b74899b0cb0f0be9671986114a}{Before\+Call\+Entered\+Callback}}}]{callback }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a callback to notify the host application right before a script is about to run. If a script re-\/enters the runtime during executing, the Before\+Call\+Entered\+Callback is invoked for each re-\/entrance. Executing scripts inside the callback will re-\/trigger the callback. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a89656ac26d523c31fbfdbb12fb32f078}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a89656ac26d523c31fbfdbb12fb32f078}}

\index{AddCallCompletedCallback@{AddCallCompletedCallback}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AddCallCompletedCallback()}{AddCallCompletedCallback()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Add\+Call\+Completed\+Callback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a87c562281d3e5dd2211344e0ce39884b}{Call\+Completed\+Callback}}}]{callback }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a callback to notify the host application when a script finished running. If a script re-\/enters the runtime during executing, the Call\+Completed\+Callback is only invoked when the outer-\/most script execution ends. Executing scripts inside the callback do not trigger further callbacks. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_abe7ab165a962dd4a944d9bc489f5d2cf}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_abe7ab165a962dd4a944d9bc489f5d2cf}}

Enables the host application to receive a notification after a garbage collection.

Enables the host application to receive a notification before a garbage collection.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em callback} & The callback to be invoked. The callback is allowed to allocate but invocation is not re-\/entrant\+: a callback triggering garbage collection will not be called again. JS execution is prohibited from these callbacks. A single callback may only be registered once. \\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AddMessageListener()}{AddMessageListener()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Add\+Message\+Listener (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a65b5d3eb0be1adaa141f01359c396c38}{Message\+Callback}}}]{callback,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}} $>$}]{data = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}}$>$()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a message listener (errors only).

The same message listener can be added more than once and in that case it will be called more than once for each message.

If data is specified, it will be passed to the callback when it is called. Otherwise, the exception object will be passed to the callback instead. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a2915583f307fd1c5084a2af4a83eeb48}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a2915583f307fd1c5084a2af4a83eeb48}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!AddMessageListenerWithErrorLevel@{AddMessageListenerWithErrorLevel}}
\index{AddMessageListenerWithErrorLevel@{AddMessageListenerWithErrorLevel}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AddMessageListenerWithErrorLevel()}{AddMessageListenerWithErrorLevel()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Add\+Message\+Listener\+With\+Error\+Level (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a65b5d3eb0be1adaa141f01359c396c38}{Message\+Callback}}}]{callback,  }\item[{int}]{message\+\_\+levels,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}} $>$}]{data = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}}$>$()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a message listener.

The same message listener can be added more than once and in that case it will be called more than once for each message.

If data is specified, it will be passed to the callback when it is called. Otherwise, the exception object will be passed to the callback instead.

A listener can listen for particular error levels by providing a mask. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_ad10bfdb01e79d7ccc850f36fc92cff81}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_ad10bfdb01e79d7ccc850f36fc92cff81}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!AddMicrotasksCompletedCallback@{AddMicrotasksCompletedCallback}}
\index{AddMicrotasksCompletedCallback@{AddMicrotasksCompletedCallback}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AddMicrotasksCompletedCallback()}{AddMicrotasksCompletedCallback()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Add\+Microtasks\+Completed\+Callback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a4a46aa0cc2b3034a9fe098fbf2ed7bfa}{Microtasks\+Completed\+Callback\+With\+Data}}}]{callback,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{data = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{flag-definitions_8h_aca14fbede0905858c819226fce3678cc}{nullptr}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a callback to notify the host application after microtasks were run on the default \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1MicrotaskQueue}{Microtask\+Queue}}. The callback is triggered by explicit Run\+Microtasks call or automatic microtasks execution (see Set\+Microtask\+Policy).

Callback will trigger even if microtasks were attempted to run, but the microtasks queue was empty and no single microtask was actually executed.

Executing scripts inside the callback will not re-\/trigger microtasks and the callback. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_ae6fc7e1186beb40707180dd58456f741}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_ae6fc7e1186beb40707180dd58456f741}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!AddNearHeapLimitCallback@{AddNearHeapLimitCallback}}
\index{AddNearHeapLimitCallback@{AddNearHeapLimitCallback}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AddNearHeapLimitCallback()}{AddNearHeapLimitCallback()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Add\+Near\+Heap\+Limit\+Callback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_aa1fc7d6f7736e8256fc03c4b3ebaf6eb}{v8\+::\+Near\+Heap\+Limit\+Callback}}}]{callback,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{data }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Add a callback to invoke in case the heap size is close to the heap limit. If multiple callbacks are added, only the most recently added callback is invoked. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_aaeda5fa60961a3d9d476c46200e30711}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_aaeda5fa60961a3d9d476c46200e30711}}

\index{AdjustAmountOfExternalAllocatedMemory@{AdjustAmountOfExternalAllocatedMemory}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}

Adjusts the amount of registered external memory.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a1f944c1aa3c0f57910a081505d01d099}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a1f944c1aa3c0f57910a081505d01d099}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!Allocate@{Allocate}}
\index{Allocate@{Allocate}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Allocate()}{Allocate()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} $\ast$ v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Allocate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Allocates a new isolate but does not initialize it. Does not change the currently entered isolate.

Only \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_aed85b3c82bf69a60ecebc2558ab95083}{Isolate\+::\+Get\+Data()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_a2ae968a7ff8a397f1ac09d32990883f6}{Isolate\+::\+Set\+Data()}}, which access the embedder-\/controlled parts of the isolate, as well as \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_ae786760e5ab4cb113fc8f097b90f827d}{Isolate\+::\+Get\+Group()}}, are allowed to be called on the uninitialized isolate. To initialize the isolate, call {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_ad26be373ae4f11e8204c01434f057add}{Isolate\+::\+Initialize()}}} or initialize a {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1SnapshotCreator}{Snapshot\+Creator}}}.

When an isolate is no longer used its resources should be freed by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_a1a5a5762e4221aff8c6b10f9e3cec0af}{Dispose()}}. Using the delete operator is not allowed.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8_ac731f26923fe216c0bcc297a49ac9266}{V8\+::\+Initialize()}} must have run prior to this. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a532b273a1164717e82f3e4be077c0f9a}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a532b273a1164717e82f3e4be077c0f9a}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!Allocate@{Allocate}}
\index{Allocate@{Allocate}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Allocate()}{Allocate()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} $\ast$ v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Allocate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1IsolateGroup}{Isolate\+Group}} \&}]{group }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_ad2ce781a7ee2bc64d6acc941d2cd24cf}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_ad2ce781a7ee2bc64d6acc941d2cd24cf}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!AutomaticallyRestoreInitialHeapLimit@{AutomaticallyRestoreInitialHeapLimit}}
\index{AutomaticallyRestoreInitialHeapLimit@{AutomaticallyRestoreInitialHeapLimit}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AutomaticallyRestoreInitialHeapLimit()}{AutomaticallyRestoreInitialHeapLimit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Automatically\+Restore\+Initial\+Heap\+Limit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{threshold\+\_\+percent = {\ttfamily 0.5} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

If the heap limit was changed by the Near\+Heap\+Limit\+Callback, then the initial heap limit will be restored once the heap size falls below the given threshold percentage of the initial heap limit. The threshold percentage is a number in (0.\+0, 1.\+0) range. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a75cbe037e7657a7c7bd65e2edf0164d5}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a75cbe037e7657a7c7bd65e2edf0164d5}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!CancelTerminateExecution@{CancelTerminateExecution}}
\index{CancelTerminateExecution@{CancelTerminateExecution}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CancelTerminateExecution()}{CancelTerminateExecution()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Cancel\+Terminate\+Execution (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Resume execution capability in the given isolate, whose execution was previously forcefully terminated using \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_ad212b2e0b66ff5d586cd79cfa0b555fb}{Terminate\+Execution()}}.

When execution is forcefully terminated using \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_ad212b2e0b66ff5d586cd79cfa0b555fb}{Terminate\+Execution()}}, the isolate can not resume execution until all Java\+Script frames have propagated the uncatchable exception which is generated. This method allows the program embedding the engine to handle the termination event and resume execution capability, even if Java\+Script frames remain on the stack.

This method can be used by any thread even if that thread has not acquired the \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} lock with a \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Locker}{Locker}} object. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_afc54f743a425d213dbc4fe119134a88c}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_afc54f743a425d213dbc4fe119134a88c}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!ClearCachesForTesting@{ClearCachesForTesting}}
\index{ClearCachesForTesting@{ClearCachesForTesting}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ClearCachesForTesting()}{ClearCachesForTesting()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Clear\+Caches\+For\+Testing (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Drop non-\/essential caches. Should only be called from testing code. The method can potentially block for a long time and does not necessarily trigger GC. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a307d8d1ca02f4d2a5c4bf29cc707ae07}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a307d8d1ca02f4d2a5c4bf29cc707ae07}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!ClearKeptObjects@{ClearKeptObjects}}
\index{ClearKeptObjects@{ClearKeptObjects}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ClearKeptObjects()}{ClearKeptObjects()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Clear\+Kept\+Objects (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Clears the set of objects held strongly by the heap. This set of objects are originally built when a Weak\+Ref is created or successfully dereferenced.

This is invoked automatically after microtasks are run. See Microtasks\+Policy for when microtasks are run.

This needs to be manually invoked only if the embedder is manually running microtasks via a custom \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1MicrotaskQueue}{Microtask\+Queue}} class\textquotesingle{}s Perform\+Checkpoint. In that case, it is the embedder\textquotesingle{}s responsibility to make this call at a time which does not interrupt synchronous ECMAScript code execution. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a4b5216bbb1792211422aee575d02f442}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a4b5216bbb1792211422aee575d02f442}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!ContextDisposedNotification@{ContextDisposedNotification}}
\index{ContextDisposedNotification@{ContextDisposedNotification}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ContextDisposedNotification()}{ContextDisposedNotification()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Context\+Disposed\+Notification (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{dependant\+\_\+context = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{flag-definitions_8h_ae56df915684f69fc6f5c0f3bd3b3c80c}{true}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Optional notification that a context has been disposed. \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} uses these notifications to guide the GC heuristic and cancel Finalization\+Registry cleanup tasks. Returns the number of context disposals -\/ including this one
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item since the last time \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} had a chance to clean up.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The optional parameter $\vert$dependant\+\_\+context$\vert$ specifies whether the disposed context was depending on state from other contexts or not. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a4e05bf5347f4f9ac3f8357147ca9f4b2}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a4e05bf5347f4f9ac3f8357147ca9f4b2}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!ContextDisposedNotification@{ContextDisposedNotification}}
\index{ContextDisposedNotification@{ContextDisposedNotification}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ContextDisposedNotification()}{ContextDisposedNotification()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Context\+Disposed\+Notification (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a4c253cc9b41dad8e3b1ce1aa7a2dbe0c}{Context\+Dependants}}}]{dependants }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Optional notification that a context has been disposed. \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} uses these notifications to guide heuristics on e.\+g. GC or compilers.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dependants} & A signal on whether this context possibly had any dependants. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a47db07c61e758522e800511517b25e6b}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a47db07c61e758522e800511517b25e6b}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!CopyCodePages@{CopyCodePages}}
\index{CopyCodePages@{CopyCodePages}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CopyCodePages()}{CopyCodePages()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Copy\+Code\+Pages (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{capacity,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structv8_1_1MemoryRange}{Memory\+Range}} $\ast$}]{code\+\_\+pages\+\_\+out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies the code heap pages currently in use by \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} into $\vert$code\+\_\+pages\+\_\+out$\vert$. $\vert$code\+\_\+pages\+\_\+out$\vert$ must have at least k\+Min\+Code\+Pages\+Buffer\+Size capacity and must be empty.

Signal-\/safe, does not allocate, does not access the \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} heap. No code on the stack can rely on pages that might be missing.

Returns the number of pages available to be copied, which might be greater than $\vert$capacity$\vert$. In this case, only $\vert$capacity$\vert$ pages will be copied into $\vert$code\+\_\+pages\+\_\+out$\vert$. The caller should provide a bigger buffer on the next call in order to get all available code pages, but this is not required. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a80a684ac76056a4ba4e3b365ca65b9ab}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a80a684ac76056a4ba4e3b365ca65b9ab}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!DateTimeConfigurationChangeNotification@{DateTimeConfigurationChangeNotification}}
\index{DateTimeConfigurationChangeNotification@{DateTimeConfigurationChangeNotification}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{DateTimeConfigurationChangeNotification()}{DateTimeConfigurationChangeNotification()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Date\+Time\+Configuration\+Change\+Notification (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_a57dcf1e56d6498b7426ef7a489454ffe}{Time\+Zone\+Detection}}}]{time\+\_\+zone\+\_\+detection = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_a57dcf1e56d6498b7426ef7a489454ffeac88bd8ce07240b0611d5ae619c1aa088}{Time\+Zone\+Detection\+::k\+Skip}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Notification that the embedder has changed the time zone, daylight savings time or other date / time configuration parameters. \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} keeps a cache of various values used for date / time computation. This notification will reset those cached values for the current context so that date / time configuration changes would be reflected.

This API should not be called more than needed as it will negatively impact the performance of date operations. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a334078bb8895660065653d4e66a82ede}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a334078bb8895660065653d4e66a82ede}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!Deinitialize@{Deinitialize}}
\index{Deinitialize@{Deinitialize}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Deinitialize()}{Deinitialize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Deinitialize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Deinitializes the isolate, but does not free the address. The isolate must not be entered by any thread to be deinitializable. Embedders must call \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_ac5de29df16ca8a5b945b95a0f4268306}{Isolate\+::\+Free()}} to free the isolate afterwards. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_ac62ff53be40f5ecd74fc9e72451da115}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_ac62ff53be40f5ecd74fc9e72451da115}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!DiscardThreadSpecificMetadata@{DiscardThreadSpecificMetadata}}
\index{DiscardThreadSpecificMetadata@{DiscardThreadSpecificMetadata}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{DiscardThreadSpecificMetadata()}{DiscardThreadSpecificMetadata()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Discard\+Thread\+Specific\+Metadata (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Discards all \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} thread-\/specific data for the \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}}. Should be used if a thread is terminating and it has used an \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} that will outlive the thread -- all thread-\/specific data for an \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} is discarded when an \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} is disposed so this call is pointless if an \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} is about to be Disposed. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a1a5a5762e4221aff8c6b10f9e3cec0af}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a1a5a5762e4221aff8c6b10f9e3cec0af}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!Dispose@{Dispose}}
\index{Dispose@{Dispose}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Dispose()}{Dispose()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Dispose (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Deinitializes and frees the isolate. The isolate must not be entered by any thread to be disposable. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a64546846b6d7f33f464ffd2006d88b93}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a64546846b6d7f33f464ffd2006d88b93}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Dump\+And\+Reset\+Stats (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Dumps activated low-\/level \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} internal stats. This can be used instead of performing a full isolate disposal. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a79a222a1a662d08479d5a1880c6793c5}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a79a222a1a662d08479d5a1880c6793c5}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!EnqueueMicrotask@{EnqueueMicrotask}}

Enqueues the callback to the default \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1MicrotaskQueue}{Microtask\+Queue}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_ae5346307ae19a641f9ee7752944daf88}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_ae5346307ae19a641f9ee7752944daf88}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{EnqueueMicrotask()}{EnqueueMicrotask()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Enqueue\+Microtask (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a1bf95eb194aa2d70f80cd148bff2def5}{Microtask\+Callback}}}]{callback,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{data = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{flag-definitions_8h_aca14fbede0905858c819226fce3678cc}{nullptr}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enqueues the callback to the default \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1MicrotaskQueue}{Microtask\+Queue}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_aec80bb49b6b7647ff75e8f2cc9484ea3}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_aec80bb49b6b7647ff75e8f2cc9484ea3}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!Enter@{Enter}}
\index{Enter@{Enter}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Enter()}{Enter()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Enter (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Methods below this point require holding a lock (using \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Locker}{Locker}}) in a multi-\/threaded environment. Sets this isolate as the entered one for the current thread. Saves the previously entered one (if any), so that it can be restored when exiting. Re-\/entering an isolate is allowed. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a64a8503cafd00d1d2cadfbb0c2345054}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a64a8503cafd00d1d2cadfbb0c2345054}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!Exit@{Exit}}
\index{Exit@{Exit}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Exit()}{Exit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Exit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Exits this isolate by restoring the previously entered one in the current thread. The isolate may still stay the same, if it was entered more than once.

Requires\+: this == \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_afd8c10d0f01e2ae43522c3ddf0bb053d}{Isolate\+::\+Get\+Current()}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_ac5de29df16ca8a5b945b95a0f4268306}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_ac5de29df16ca8a5b945b95a0f4268306}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!Free@{Free}}
\index{Free@{Free}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Free()}{Free()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Free (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} $\ast$}]{isolate }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Frees the memory allocated for the isolate. Can only be called after the \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} has already been deinitialized with \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_a334078bb8895660065653d4e66a82ede}{Isolate\+::\+Deinitialize()}}. After the isolate is freed, the next call to \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_abab88b427984481cb58c371f6cb30005}{Isolate\+::\+New()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_a1f944c1aa3c0f57910a081505d01d099}{Isolate\+::\+Allocate()}} might return the same address that just get freed. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_afdb09b8a5203040b2921847290104da2}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_afdb09b8a5203040b2921847290104da2}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!Freeze@{Freeze}}
\index{Freeze@{Freeze}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Freeze()}{Freeze()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Freeze (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{is\+\_\+frozen }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Optional notification to tell \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} whether the embedder is currently frozen. \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} uses these notifications to guide heuristics. This is an unfinished experimental feature. Semantics and implementation may change frequently. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_af26459092934b9b20ef5f7551634a5c2}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_af26459092934b9b20ef5f7551634a5c2}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!GetArrayBufferAllocator@{GetArrayBufferAllocator}}
\index{GetArrayBufferAllocator@{GetArrayBufferAllocator}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetArrayBufferAllocator()}{GetArrayBufferAllocator()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1ArrayBuffer_1_1Allocator}{Array\+Buffer\+::\+Allocator}} $\ast$ v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Get\+Array\+Buffer\+Allocator (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1ArrayBuffer_1_1Allocator}{Array\+Buffer\+::\+Allocator}} used in this isolate. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a46c7fb2282970530c32740d7e5999b22}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a46c7fb2282970530c32740d7e5999b22}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!GetCodeRange@{GetCodeRange}}
\index{GetCodeRange@{GetCodeRange}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetCodeRange()}{GetCodeRange()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Get\+Code\+Range (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$$\ast$}]{start,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{length\+\_\+in\+\_\+bytes }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a memory range that can potentially contain jitted code. Code for \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}}\textquotesingle{}s \textquotesingle{}builtins\textquotesingle{} will not be in this range if embedded builtins is enabled.

On Win64, embedders are advised to install function table callbacks for these ranges, as default SEH won\textquotesingle{}t be able to unwind through jitted code. The first page of the code range is reserved for the embedder and is committed, writable, and executable, to be used to store unwind data, as documented in \href{https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/cpp/build/exception-handling-x64}{\texttt{ https\+://docs.\+microsoft.\+com/en-\/us/cpp/build/exception-\/handling-\/x64}}.

Might be empty on other platforms.

\href{https://code.google.com/p/v8/issues/detail?id=3598}{\texttt{ https\+://code.\+google.\+com/p/v8/issues/detail?id=3598}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_ad77e28282e505783f930f3cd2d096804}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_ad77e28282e505783f930f3cd2d096804}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!GetContinuationPreservedEmbedderData@{GetContinuationPreservedEmbedderData}}
\index{GetContinuationPreservedEmbedderData@{GetContinuationPreservedEmbedderData}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetContinuationPreservedEmbedderData()}{GetContinuationPreservedEmbedderData()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}} $>$ v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Get\+Continuation\+Preserved\+Embedder\+Data (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the value that was set or restored by \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_adddfd7d277fc0d31e6ad023aeb957e86}{Set\+Continuation\+Preserved\+Embedder\+Data()}}, if any. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_ace5a7f4d4103bf636ce6ac7ce9c30851}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_ace5a7f4d4103bf636ce6ac7ce9c30851}}

\index{LocaleConfigurationChangeNotification@{LocaleConfigurationChangeNotification}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{LocaleConfigurationChangeNotification()}{LocaleConfigurationChangeNotification()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Locale\+Configuration\+Change\+Notification (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Notification that the embedder has changed the locale. \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} keeps a cache of various values used for locale computation. This notification will reset those cached values for the current context so that locale configuration changes would be reflected.

This API should not be called more than needed as it will negatively impact the performance of locale operations. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_aaf446f4877e4707a93d2c406fffd9fd6}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_aaf446f4877e4707a93d2c406fffd9fd6}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Measure\+Memory (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1MeasureMemoryDelegate}{Measure\+Memory\+Delegate}} $>$}]{delegate,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_ae7d05bf926fdcef988b14900496ea931}{Measure\+Memory\+Execution}}}]{execution = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_ae7d05bf926fdcef988b14900496ea931a6867faeaa475fda467e48267db2bb8a8}{Measure\+Memory\+Execution\+::k\+Default}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This API is experimental and may change significantly.

Enqueues a memory measurement request and invokes the delegate with the results.

Optional notification that the system is running low on memory. \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} uses these notifications to guide heuristics. \index{New@{New}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{New()}{New()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} $\ast$ v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+New (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structv8_1_1Isolate_1_1CreateParams}{Create\+Params}} \&}]{params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Creates a new isolate. Does not change the currently entered isolate.

When an isolate is no longer used its resources should be freed by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_a1a5a5762e4221aff8c6b10f9e3cec0af}{Dispose()}}. Using the delete operator is not allowed.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8_ac731f26923fe216c0bcc297a49ac9266}{V8\+::\+Initialize()}} must have run prior to this. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a3840e2a1041601514ae074133dc65f5e}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a3840e2a1041601514ae074133dc65f5e}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Perform\+Microtask\+Checkpoint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Runs the default \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1MicrotaskQueue}{Microtask\+Queue}} until it gets empty and perform other microtask checkpoint steps, such as calling Clear\+Kept\+Objects. Asserts that the Microtasks\+Policy is not k\+Scoped. Any exceptions thrown by microtask callbacks are swallowed. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a92be6cf5ce1e7360843794cc1528369f}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a92be6cf5ce1e7360843794cc1528369f}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Remove\+Near\+Heap\+Limit\+Callback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_aa1fc7d6f7736e8256fc03c4b3ebaf6eb}{v8\+::\+Near\+Heap\+Limit\+Callback}}}]{callback,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{heap\+\_\+limit }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Remove the given callback and restore the heap limit to the given limit. If the given limit is zero, then it is ignored. If the current heap size is greater than the given limit, then the heap limit is restored to the minimal limit that is possible for the current heap size. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a59fe893ed7e9df52cef2d59b2d98ab23}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a59fe893ed7e9df52cef2d59b2d98ab23}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Request\+Garbage\+Collection\+For\+Testing (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_a5ae00cc99d8aca148c6f5f9698c432c9}{Garbage\+Collection\+Type}}}]{type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Request garbage collection in this \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}}. It is only valid to call this function if --expose\+\_\+gc was specified.

This should only be used for testing purposes and not to enforce a garbage collection schedule. It has strong negative impact on the garbage collection performance. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate_ae1b8d5696ba55dd3412989811c44c373}{Memory\+Pressure\+Notification()}} instead to influence the garbage collection schedule. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a2f770f6863e8bb7951eead037bb634e9}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a2f770f6863e8bb7951eead037bb634e9}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{RequestInterrupt()}{RequestInterrupt()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Request\+Interrupt (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a77f4f48839bdd54ba1f9f2316d0130b4}{Interrupt\+Callback}}}]{callback,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{data }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Request \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} to interrupt long running Java\+Script code and invoke the given $\vert$callback$\vert$ passing the given $\vert$data$\vert$ to it. After $\vert$callback$\vert$ returns control will be returned to the Java\+Script code. There may be a number of interrupt requests in flight. Can be called from another thread without acquiring a $\vert$\+Locker$\vert$. Registered $\vert$callback$\vert$ must not reenter interrupted \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_abb10c6229576e34ae1e8ca1d4d65312e}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_abb10c6229576e34ae1e8ca1d4d65312e}}

\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!SetIsLoading@{SetIsLoading}}
\index{SetIsLoading@{SetIsLoading}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SetIsLoading()}{SetIsLoading()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Set\+Is\+Loading (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{is\+\_\+loading }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Optional notification to tell \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} whether the embedder is currently loading resources. If the embedder uses this notification, it should call Set\+Is\+Loading(true) when loading starts and Set\+Is\+Loading(false) when it ends. It\textquotesingle{}s valid to call Set\+Is\+Loading(true) again while loading, which will update the timestamp when \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} considers the load started. Calling Set\+Is\+Loading(false) while not loading does nothing. \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} uses these notifications to guide heuristics. This is an unfinished experimental feature. Semantics and implementation may change frequently. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a71d976355bf47eb2dd09cd5d1279a40d}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a71d976355bf47eb2dd09cd5d1279a40d}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!SetJitCodeEventHandler@{SetJitCodeEventHandler}}
\index{SetJitCodeEventHandler@{SetJitCodeEventHandler}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SetJitCodeEventHandler()}{SetJitCodeEventHandler()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Set\+Jit\+Code\+Event\+Handler (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a06f34fa4fa4cfc8518366808d1d461c1}{Jit\+Code\+Event\+Options}}}]{options,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a02866fcd282824464e1bc83dbdbfb0c2}{Jit\+Code\+Event\+Handler}}}]{event\+\_\+handler }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Allows the host application to provide the address of a function that is notified each time code is added, moved or removed.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em options} & options for the JIT code event handler. \\
\hline
{\em event\+\_\+handler} & the JIT code event handler, which will be invoked each time code is added, moved or removed. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
{\ttfamily event\+\_\+handler} won\textquotesingle{}t get notified of existent code. 

since code removal notifications are not currently issued, the {\ttfamily event\+\_\+handler} may get notifications of code that overlaps earlier code notifications. This happens when code areas are reused, and the earlier overlapping code areas should therefore be discarded. 

the events passed to {\ttfamily event\+\_\+handler} and the strings they point to are not guaranteed to live past each call. The {\ttfamily event\+\_\+handler} must copy strings and other parameters it needs to keep around. 

the set of events declared in \mbox{\hyperlink{structv8_1_1JitCodeEvent_ac4f8e391762567a2710eb5552b5f11f7}{Jit\+Code\+Event\+::\+Event\+Type}} is expected to grow over time, and the \mbox{\hyperlink{structv8_1_1JitCodeEvent}{Jit\+Code\+Event}} structure is expected to accrue new members. The {\ttfamily event\+\_\+handler} function must ignore event codes it does not recognize to maintain future compatibility. 

Use \mbox{\hyperlink{structv8_1_1Isolate_1_1CreateParams}{Isolate\+::\+Create\+Params}} to get events for code executed during \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} setup. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a5ab1b6781491ff6ea431a2adfcce2afe}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a5ab1b6781491ff6ea431a2adfcce2afe}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!SetMemorySaverMode@{SetMemorySaverMode}}
\index{SetMemorySaverMode@{SetMemorySaverMode}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SetMemorySaverMode()}{SetMemorySaverMode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Set\+Memory\+Saver\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{memory\+\_\+saver\+\_\+mode\+\_\+enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Optional request from the embedder to tune \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8}{v8}} towards memory efficiency rather than speed if {\ttfamily memory\+\_\+saver\+\_\+mode\+\_\+enabled} is true, because the embedder is in memory saver mode. If false, the correct tuning is left to \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8}{v8}} to decide. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_ae19bd6443174d5ed666132606d55d0be}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_ae19bd6443174d5ed666132606d55d0be}}

Enables the host application to provide a mechanism for recording event based metrics. In order to use this interface include/v8-\/metrics.\+h needs to be included and the recorder needs to be derived from the Recorder base class defined there. {\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Terminate\+Execution (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Forcefully terminate the current thread of Java\+Script execution in the given isolate.

This method can be used by any thread even if that thread has not acquired the \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1V8}{V8}} lock with a \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Locker}{Locker}} object. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a630166a6a770ece436ebcea8f27e8da8}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a630166a6a770ece436ebcea8f27e8da8}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$int N$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}}$>$ v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Throw\+Error (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char(\&)}]{message\mbox{[}\+N\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Schedules a \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Exception_a67c28710ee5681066d04cfcd21544827}{v8\+::\+Exception\+::\+Error}} with the given message. See Throw\+Exception for more details. Templatized to provide compile-\/time errors in case of too long strings (see \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1String_a7173d65b0e50225bf63d98d179b9821c}{v8\+::\+String\+::\+New\+From\+Utf8\+Literal}}). \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a0871772c55da6c529761abd0378fc8c7}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a0871772c55da6c529761abd0378fc8c7}}

\index{ThrowException@{ThrowException}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ThrowException()}{ThrowException()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{v8\+::\+Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}} $>$ v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Throw\+Exception (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}} $>$}]{exception }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Schedules an exception to be thrown when returning to Java\+Script. When an exception has been scheduled it is illegal to invoke any Java\+Script operation; the caller must return immediately and only after the exception has been handled does it become legal to invoke Java\+Script operations. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_aa672f933a7881431b14362489d42192f}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_aa672f933a7881431b14362489d42192f}}

\index{TryGetCurrent@{TryGetCurrent}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} $\ast$ v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Try\+Get\+Current (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Returns the entered isolate for the current thread or NULL in case there is no current isolate.

No checks are performed by this method. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Isolate_a2d71818254388e739462bd3e06a2fa99}\label{classv8_1_1Isolate_a2d71818254388e739462bd3e06a2fa99}} 
\index{v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}!ValidateAndCanonicalizeUnicodeLocaleId@{ValidateAndCanonicalizeUnicodeLocaleId}}
\index{ValidateAndCanonicalizeUnicodeLocaleId@{ValidateAndCanonicalizeUnicodeLocaleId}!v8::Isolate@{v8::Isolate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ValidateAndCanonicalizeUnicodeLocaleId()}{ValidateAndCanonicalizeUnicodeLocaleId()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Maybe}{Maybe}}$<$ std\+::string $>$ v8\+::\+Isolate\+::\+Validate\+And\+Canonicalize\+Unicode\+Locale\+Id (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::string\+\_\+view}]{locale }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a canonical and case-\/regularized form of locale if Intl support is enabled. If the locale is not syntactically well-\/formed, throws a Range\+Error.

If Intl support is not enabled, returns \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_ada000f8d5f1f65a26be3b35f8f398d28}{Nothing$<$std\+::string$>$()}}.

Corresponds to the combination of the abstract operations Is\+Structurally\+Valid\+Language\+Tag and Canonicalize\+Unicode\+Locale\+Id. See\+: \href{https://tc39.es/ecma402/\#sec-isstructurallyvalidlanguagetag}{\texttt{ https\+://tc39.\+es/ecma402/\#sec-\/isstructurallyvalidlanguagetag}} \href{https://tc39.es/ecma402/\#sec-canonicalizeunicodelocaleid}{\texttt{ https\+://tc39.\+es/ecma402/\#sec-\/canonicalizeunicodelocaleid}}
